_*/Taylor v. Google/**/LLC/**, [PERSON]*_

There has been a Settlement in a class action lawsuit called /Taylor v. 
Google//LLC/, Case No. 5:20-cv-07956-VKD (N.D. Cal.) (Б─°LawsuitБ─²), and 
you may be a class member. The Court authorized this Notice because you 
have a right to know about the Settlement, before the Court decides 
whether to approve it.

Your rights may be affected. Please read this Notice carefully.

*What is the **L**awsuit about?*

The Plaintiffs allege that GoogleБ─≥s Android operating system causes 
Android mobile devices to transfer a variety of information to Google 
without usersБ─≥ permission, consuming usersБ─≥ cellular data from their 
cellular data plans. Plaintiffs allege that certain transfers occur in 
the background, without any notice to the user, including when the 
devices are in a completely idle state, meaning they are not in use or 
being touched, with all apps closed. Plaintiffs allege that even though 
Google could make it so that these transfers happen only when the 
devices are connected to Wi-Fi, Google instead causes these transfers to 
sometimes take place over a cellular network. Plaintiffs allege that 
GoogleБ─≥s unauthorized use of their cellular data violates the law and 
requires Google to compensate Plaintiffs for the value of the cellular 
data that Google used for its own benefit without their permission.

Google denies the claims in this Lawsuit and that it did anything wrong. 
The Court has not made a determination regarding PlaintiffsБ─≥ allegations.

*Who is **I**ncluded?*

The [PERSON] includes all natural persons in the [PERSON], 
who have used mobile devices running the Android operating system to 
access the internet through cellular data networks operated by mobile 
carriers, at any time from November 12, 2017 to the date this Settlement 
receives final approval, excluding persons who are class members in 
/Csupo v. Google //LLC/ 
<https://t3kzfhdh.r.us-east-1.awstrack.me/L0/https:%2F%2Fcellulardataclassaction.com%2Fhome/1/0100019d5420e8e0-eb022324-2ced-41cb-acb5-f327b2d9b099-000000/LJqDgmrfkB8un4Oaj43OMvX0--o=472>, 
[PERSON], No. 19CV352557, a similar lawsuit 
involving residents of California.

The [PERSON] does _not_ include:

  * Google and GoogleБ─≥s subsidiaries and affiliates, officers, and
    directors;
  * The judge(s) to whom these cases are or have been assigned and any
    member of the judgeБ─≥s or judgesБ─≥ immediate family;
  * [PERSON];
  * Anyone that excludes themselves from the [PERSON]; and
  * [PERSON] in the lawsuit /Csupo v. Google/ /LLC/, [PERSON], No. 19CV352557.

*What **D**oes the Settlement **P**rovide?*

The Settlement has the following key terms:

  * Google will pay $135 million.
  * Google will be required to update the [PERSON] of Service,
    a page in GoogleБ─≥s [PERSON] website, and the setup screens that
    are shown to Android users during device setup. These updates will
    disclose the conduct at issue in the Lawsuit to Android users and
    ask them to consent to it. Google will also disable a related
    setting on Android devices.
  * The Plaintiffs and Class will release all claims against Google that
    were asserted or could have been asserted in this Lawsuit, as
    specified in the [PERSON].

If the Settlement is approved by the Court, the [PERSON] will be 
used to pay money to eligible [PERSON] (/i.e.,/ 
[PERSON] who do not opt out of the Settlement); notice 
and administration costs; attorneysБ─≥ fees, costs, and expenses; service 
awards to the [PERSON]; and any taxes incurred by the 
[PERSON].


The full text of the [PERSON], as well as the proposed 
updates to the [PERSON] of Service, [PERSON] website, and 
Android setup screens are available on the LawsuitБ─≥s website,

  Tip #2 - How to get reservations


    Attract the students with your Tutor's profile


Dear teacher,

In order to upgrade your [PERSON], besides opening available slots, 
you also need to attract students to choose you and book your slots. 
Now, we will talk about your [PERSON]. If you have an 
attractive and teasing profile, you will be more interesting for 
students to choose exactly you as their teacher.


      Tips for the self-introduction text:

Use *simple sentences*, so the students can easily understand them.
Write something about your educational background and experience so the 
students can be introduced to *your basic background*.
Write *why do you like this job* and some of your interests.
Use the end of the introduction to write them *what benefits they will 
have by choosing you* for their classes.


      Tips for the introduction video:

*Introduce yourself* at the beginning and say something basic about 
yourself.
Tell the students *why you love this job* and mention your interests.
Mention *the benefits of having you* as their teacher.
Make your own video! *Be unique!*


Students also read the feedback from other students, so try your best to 
be a great teacher, so the students leave you excellent and valuable 
reviews.

[PERSON] forward to continuing having you as one of our teachers!

Best regards,

[PERSON], You're a week out from Decision Day. Your inbox is full, your 
parents have opinions, and you're likely wondering:/is this going to be 
worth it? Is this the right place for me?/

These are completely valid questions to ask. Student debt is real. AI is

school is starting to feel like a *very expensive gamble.*

[PERSON]


  Tip #3 - How to get reservations


    Add textbook badges to attract more students


Dear teacher,

We are sending you these tips in order to help you to get more 
reservations as this is one of the conditions to get the higher [PERSON] in the future. There are various students who want to study 
different lessons, so we would recommend you to request as many badges 
as it is available to have.
*In this way, you will increase the chances to get more regular students 
and Booked lessons with them.*

Native CampNative CampNative CampNative CampNative Camp


      If you donБ─≥t have a badge of the lesson which a student is looking
      for at the moment, a student will not be able to book your slots
      or to have lessons with you for the certain topic.

TeacherБ─≥s available badges can be found on your public profile page for 
students (example: https://nativecamp.net/waiting/detail/xxxx 
<https://nativecamp.net/waiting/detail/xxxx>, where "xxxx" is your 
Teacher ID)

Teaching material badges are awarded to the teachers who have requested 
them and passed the specified qualifications for badges.

In order to have a good feedback from your students and quality lessons 
please be aware that if you request the badge, you need to get familiar 
with the lesson material and the lesson flow, to be well-prepared before 
you start conducting lessons to your students.

[PERSON] forward to continuing having you as one of our teachers!

Best regards,
[PERSON]

*LUCKY TOKYO* is loud, layered, slightly chaotic, and impossible to 
ignore Б─■ exactly as intended. It takes the kind of visual overload that 
makes Tokyo feel alive and turns it into something you can carry every 
day on your phone, laptop, tablet, console, or whatever device in your 
life currently looks far too plain.


At the centre of it all is the *Maneki-neko* Б─■ _the lucky cat_. A small 
symbol with a big reputation. In Japanese culture, it is tied to good 
fortune, prosperity, and welcome. We liked the idea of taking that 
energy and dropping it straight onto your everyday tech. Not in a subtle 
way. In a *why-is-my-device-suddenly-this-cool* way.


But this design is not just one symbol doing all the work.

Look closer and it starts unfolding.

<https://pkr.soundestlink.com/ce/c/675ca4d10bb04571bef4b25b/69d66d892f73c84b91148ef0/69d66dd641d31987815af16e?signature=5efd3782d81e94feae8d4fc3929ebb31a762c591c5d9b99c6f2be01ab1bce2ab> 


There is the calm face of a traditional doll sitting right next to the 
drama of a kabuki mask. Koi cut through the composition like movement 
made visible. Butterflies, florals, waves, street signs, food-box 
details Б─■ every part adds to the sense that this skin did not come from 
a boardroom trying to look tasteful. It came from a love of contrast, 
clutter, symbolism, and cities that never ask permission to have 
personality.


That is what makes *LUCKY TOKYO* work.

It is busy, but not messy. Playful, but not childish. Bold, but still 
precise. The kind of design that keeps giving you something new to 
notice every time you pick up your device. A little luck here. A little 
attitude there. A lot of character everywhere else.


_We made it because not everyone wants clean and quiet._


Sometimes you want a design with pulse.
Something with stories in it.
Something that feels collected rather than decorated.
Something that looks like it has actually lived.

<https://pkr.soundestlink.com/ce/c/675ca4d10bb04571bef4b25b/69d66d892f73c84b91148ef0/69d66dd641d31987815af16f?signature=5efd3782d81e94feae8d4fc3929ebb31a762c591c5d9b99c6f2be01ab1bce2ab> 


And yes, it works across *smartphones, laptops, tablets, game consoles, 
and more* Б─■ because a design this alive should not have to stop at one 
device.


So no, we are not saying a skin can change your life.


But we are saying your device could look a lot luckier.

[PERSON]


  Tip #1 - How to get reservations


    Open your slots as much as possible


Dear teacher,

We would like to share some tips on how to have more Booked lessons in 
order to earn more and upgrade your [PERSON]. One of the conditions to 
upgrade the [PERSON] is to have a certain number of Booked lessons.


      Make your schedule available!

[PERSON]

* This sheet is just an example to show you how it looks like when a 
teacher has most of available slots.


    QUESTION: When can students book your slot?

ANSWER: When you open available slots, students can choose the time to 
book you as their teacher.


    [PERSON]: How many slots do you need to open in order to have Booked
    lessons?

ANSWER: We advise you to think about your week schedule in advance and 
to open all slots at your available time in order to get more 
reservations from students. There is no exact number of slots you need 
to open. As more you open slots as more you will have opportunities to 
be booked.


      [PERSON] be careful while opening slots because of the cancellation policy 
(do not open slots if you are not sure you will be available in that 
period).

[PERSON]

/*We still encourage you to be more active, open slots and have more 
Booked lessons because we would like you to have the opportunity to be 
upgraded with your next [PERSON] while at the same time our students 
can book our best teachers. * /

Looking forward to continuing having you as one of our teachers!

Best regards,
[PERSON]
